									}
								}

										}

country_event = {
	id = POP_Travel_Time.99
	title = POP_Travel_Time.99_t
	desc = POP_Travel_Time.99_d
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_AU_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = show_ce_info
		any_owned_province = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					is_core = ROOT
					has_construction = core
					is_colony = yes
					has_province_modifier = martial_law
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = core_province_y
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = core_province_n
				value = 0
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_core = ROOT
							has_construction = core
							is_colony = yes
							has_province_modifier = martial_law
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						unrest = 0.101
					}
					PREV = {
						change_variable = {
							which = core_province_n
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					PREV = {
						change_variable = {
							which = core_province_y
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = POP_Travel_Time.99_o1
	}
	option = {
		name = POP_Travel_Time.99_o2
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = show_ce_info
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = core_province_y
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = core_province_n
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}
